the <span class="t3 t7 t9 t10 t15 t19 t22 hoverable">truth</span> of the Self? Those who are instructed
by the knowers of T r u t h <span class="t8 t13 hoverable">become</span> undoubtedly
knowers of T r u t h themselves. Those who are
instructed by pasus are verily pasus. It is only
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> who is ' s t r u c k ' (initiated by subtle impact)
that can ' s t r i k e ' o t h e r s ; <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> who is n o t ' s t r u c k '
can hardly be the ' s t r i k e r . ' Only the liberated
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> can liberate; how indeed can the unliberated
be the liberator?
Only the proficient in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> can uplift
the foolish; how indeed can the foolish uplift
the foolish?
Only the boat can ferry the stone across:
surely a stone <span class="t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">cannot</span> ferry a stone!
Engrossed in the affairs of the world, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span>
obtains no fruit whatever either here or there,
getting a Guru w h o knows not the T r u t h .
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Three</span> are the Gurus <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">among</span> the Shaivas; five
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">among</span> the Vaishnavas; hundreds in the Vedas
and Sastras. But in the K.ula there is only <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span>
Guru.
The Gurus are of six kinds *:
* <span class="t1 t2 t18 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">Different</span> traditions have <span class="t1 t2 t18 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">different</span> classifications of
the Gurus. There is for instance <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> tradition which
speaks of twelve kinds of Gurus:
1. Dhatuvadi Guru who ensures liberation by making
the disciple practice sadhana, observances and so on.
2. Candana Guru who emanates his high consciousness <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the sandal tree giving out its fragrance and
imparting it to other trees in its environs. His mere
proximity acts for liberation.
3. Vicara Guru who acts on the <span class="t20 hoverable">intelligence</span> of the
disciple and leads him through subtler and subtler operations of the buddhi.
4. Anugraha Guru who uplifts by sheer grace.

Preraka, impeller, who impels interest that
leads to initiation; Sucaka, indicator, who
indicates the sadhana in which interest has been
awakened; Vacaka, explainer, who explains the
process and its object; Darsaka, shower, who
shows definitely the working and its aim in
greater detail; Siksaka, teacher, who actually
teaches how to do sadhana; Bodhaka, Illuminator, who lights up in the disciple the l a m p of
knowledge, mental and spiritual. Of these, the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">first</span> five are, as it were, the effects of the last as
the Cause. For it is only the understanding
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> imparted by the Bodhaka that brings
5. Parasa Guru whoso mere touch, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> that of parasa
(philosopher's stone) transmutes the disciple.
6. Kacchapa Guru who redeems the disciple merely
by thinking of him, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the Kacchapa, tortoise, nourishing its young ones by <span class="t0 t5 t6 t14 t18 hoverable">thought</span> alone.
7. Candra Guru <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span> natural rays melt the being
of the disciple in the manner of the chandrakanta stone
(moon-stone) oozing out at the rays of the moon.
8. Darpana Guru who <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> a mirror reveals the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">true</span>
<span class="t6 t7 t8 t9 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> (of yourself and the universe) when you meet him.
9. Chayanidhi Guru, <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span> mere shadow confers
divinity on you <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">even</span> as the shadow of the bird Chayanidhi
is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">said</span> to confer kinghood on whomsoever falls its
shadow.
10. Nadanidhi Guru who <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the precious stone of
that name, which transmutes any metal into gold the
moment its sound reaches it, gives <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Knowledge</span> the moment
the call of the aspirant reaches him.
11. Krauncapaksi
Guru <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span> mere remembrance
confers <span class="t7 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">spiritual</span> elevation on the disciple <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the
remembrance by the Krauncapaksi feeding its young ones
in a <span class="t6 t9 t18 t26 hoverable">far</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">away</span> place.
12. Suryakanta Guru, <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span> mere glance burns up the
sins of the disciple <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the rays of the <span class="t0 t8 t11 t14 t23 t25 t28 hoverable">sun</span> burning cotton
and the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> when they fall on it through the sun-crystal.

CHAPTER X

DIKSHA (INITIATION)*
It is laid down by the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Lord</span> that there can be
no moksa, liberation, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> diksa, initiation;
and initiation <span class="t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">cannot</span> be there <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> a Teacher,
hence it comes down the line of Teachers,
parampara.
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Without</span> a Teacher, all philosophy,
traditional knowledge, Mantras are fruitless.
Him alone the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">gods</span> laud who is the Guru
keeping active what is handed down by tradition, who is <span class="t1 t2 t4 t6 t8 t10 t12 t13 t14 t17 t19 t23 t25 t28 hoverable">well</span> versed in the Mantras and
Agamas and guards the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">way</span> of the Samaya
(Traditional) Doctrine. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Though</span> himself unattached, the Guru, after testing him for some
time, on command of the Lord, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> deliver
(the truth) to his disciple, in <span class="t0 t6 t7 t8 t11 t13 t14 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> to vest him
with authority. Of h i m who is so invested
with authority, there is verily union with the
Supreme Shiva; at the termination of the bodily
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> his is the eternal liberation - this is declared
by the Lord. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> should <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> seek with
all effort to have a Guru of the unbroken Tradition born of the supreme Shiva himself.
After testing the disciple in the prescribed
manner for the fruition of the Shakti and for
happy success, the Guru <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> communicate to
h i m the Mantra; otherwise it will be fruitless.
If <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> gives contrary to this requirement, if
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> receives contrary to it, both he who gives
and he who receives <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> stand cursed for generations. If, out of delusion, the Guru and the

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> be communicated <span class="t3 t5 t7 t9 t20 t28 t29 hoverable">whole</span> i e. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> segmenting it. i m p u r e <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the cow's milk mixed w i t h dog's

To initiate <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> who is unfit by reason of

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> and in action, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> the Guru test the
disciple with effort for the period of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> year or

such delusive cruel doings, <span class="t0 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">words</span> corresponding
to these doings, frequent partialities, indifferences, several and repeated, whether pulled or
beaten, always takes it as the Grace of the Guru.

audience, in prostration to him, in his service,
in calling him and sending him off - they are fit
to be inducted in the purification for initiation.
T h e disciple <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">also</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> test the Guru in
similar signs of joy etc. in japa, stotra, dhyana,
homa, puja and so on. After knowing his capacity for transmission of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span> perfection
in the science of Mantra, ability to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">make</span> subtle
impact, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> is to <span class="t8 t13 hoverable">become</span> his disciple, not otherwise.
There are those who are competent in the
beginning, those competent in the middle and
those competent in the end, due to the transmission of the Guru's Shakti; these disciples are
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> the lowest, the middling and the best
respectively.
Those in w h o m there is devotion at the outset, when they <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">come</span> for initiation but <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span>
enthusiasm cools down soon, are the adiyogya,
competent in the beginning.
Those who arrive when the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> for initiation is at <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t29 hoverable">hand</span> and have <span class="t4 t18 t22 hoverable">neither</span> special nor a n y
knowledge, but <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span> past is done a w a y with
by their devotion, are the madhyayogya, competent in the middle.
Those who have no devotion at the outset,
who have devotion in the middle and <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 hoverable">whose</span>
devotion is fully grown at the <span class="t7 t10 t15 t25 hoverable">end</span> are the
antayogya, competent at the <span class="t7 t10 t15 t25 hoverable">end</span> and <span class="t6 t10 t15 hoverable">known</span> as the
best jnanins.
Instruction, upadesa, is of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> k i n d s : that
of karma, of dharma, of jnana. Of these the
instruction or path of karma proceeds slowly
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the ant which takes <span class="t1 t6 t21 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">long</span> to reach the fruit
at the top of the tree, proceeding slowly and
slowly. The path of dharma is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the pace of

the monkey which strains, jumping from branch
to branch, and reaches the fruit. The path of
jnana is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> that of the bird which flies straight
and rests on the fruit quickly.
Initiation, diksa, is of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> k i n d s : initiation
by touch, spared, initiation by sight, drksanjna,
initiation by thought, manasa - all these <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span>
are done <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> ritual, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> exertion.
Initiation and instruction by touch is likened
to the slow nourishing of its young by the bird
with the w a r m t h of its wings.
Initiation and instruction by sight is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the
nourishing of its young by the fish through its
seeing alone.
Initiation and instruction by <span class="t0 t5 t6 t14 t18 hoverable">thought</span> (subtle
impingement) is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> the nourishing of its young
by the tortoise by only thinking of t h e m .
The disciple receives the Grace <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t17 t18 t19 t21 t22 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">according</span>
to the impact of the Shakti, saktipata; where
there is no impact of sakti, there is no fulfilment.
Altogether, diksa, initiation, that gives
liberation is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">said</span> to be of seven k i n d s : diksa
through r i t u a l ; through letter; through special
emanation (kala); through touch; through
speech; through s i g h t ; through thought.
Diksa is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">also</span> classified as f o l l o w s : samaya,
when it authorises the disciple to help the Guru
manually in puja etc.; putrika when it enjoins
on him to perform the ritual indicated; sadhika,
when it initiates h i m in the inner sadhana;
vedhaka, when it impinges subtly; purna-acharya
when it vests on <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> the full competence of a
teacher; nirvana, when it leads to laya through
sadhana.
Eightfold again is diksa through outer ritual

in which kunda fire-bowl, mandapa, enclosure,

to be adopted for the purification of the body.
Diksa of letter, varna is threefold depending
on whether the letters are 42 or 50 or 62 Letters
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> be placed on the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> of the disciple and
withdrawn in reverse order, joining his consciousness to the supreme Self. After withdrawal, the letters are to be again laid on the
<span class="t9 hoverable">person</span> of the disciple in the <span class="t0 t6 t7 t8 t11 t13 t14 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> of <span class="t14 hoverable">creation</span>
and as prescribed; so too <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> be exercised the
Consciousness. The state of godhood full of
delight is born in the child (of the Guru). This is
the varnamayi diksa which removes all bonds.
Kala diksa is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">also</span> threefold* to be done as
prescribed. Beginning from the base of the feet
up to the knee, it is nivrtti kala; from the knee
to the navel it is pratistha; from navel to the
neck it is vidya; from the neck to the forehead
it is santi; from there to the head it is
santyatita.
This is the graded spread of kaladiksa.
Following the <span class="t0 t6 t7 t8 t11 t13 t14 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> of withdrawal, the
knower of the sequence, joins from <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> to
<span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> up to the head. This is the kala diksa of
38 parts or 50. Knowing from the Guru, following the <span class="t0 t6 t7 t8 t11 t13 t14 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">order</span> of <span class="t14 hoverable">creation</span> and withdrawal in the
placement of the tattvas, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> center and
impinge on the disciple. Then is born the state
of godhead and the meeting with the yogins and
viras (higher beings). This is the kala diksa
which destroys the bonds of the pashu.
* anavi, sakti, sambhavi, that is to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">day</span> effectuating

Invoking <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Lord</span> Siva in the hand, doing japa
as prescribed, the Guru <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> touch the <span class="t9 hoverable">person</span>
of the disciple; this is sparSa diksa, tactual
initiation.
Securing the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> in the T r u t h , <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> the
Guru utter the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> of Mantras which are
expansions of the supreme T r u t h ; that is the
vag-diksa, verbal initiation.
Closing the eyes and meditating <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> the
supreme Truth, with a happy <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> the
Guru gaze <span class="t1 t2 t4 t6 t8 t10 t12 t13 t14 t17 t19 t23 t25 t28 hoverable">well</span> into the disciple; that is drgdiksa, ocular initiation.
When by the mere look or speech or touch
of the Guru, there is an instantaneous Knowledge, that is sambhavi diksa.
Of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">two</span> kinds is mano-diksa, mental initiation - intense and highly intense, tivra and
tivratara.
Knowing the sixfold Route, adhva,
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> <span class="t6 t7 t8 t9 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> in the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> of the disciple, the
bhuvana, tattva, kala} varna, pada and mantra from the knee, navel, heart, neck, palate to top
of the head.
The wise <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> effect the vedha (subtle
impact) following the method received from
the Guru. In a moment will the disciple in
bonds get freed from them. This is intense,
tivra, initiation yielding liberation.
Merely by remembrance on the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t17 t18 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">part</span> of the
Guru, proficient in the vedha, the disciple has
his <span class="t26 hoverable">sin</span> severed; this is the highly intense,
tivratara diksa. Released from external activity
he falls on the ground instantly; a godly state
arises in him and he comes to <span class="t0 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 hoverable">know</span> everything.
Whatever is there at that moment of impact, he
experiences it himself, but on waking up he is
unable to speak of that happiness. Struck by

such impact, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> verily is a Shiva, he has no
more birth This is the tivratara diksa that
releases from the bonds of birth, yields the
very state of Shiva.
Of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> so struck six are the states described:
joy, tremor, <span class="t0 t1 t5 t6 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t18 t19 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">new</span> birth, reeling, sleep, swoon.
These six characteristics are seen at the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">time</span> of
the impact. Wherever be the <span class="t9 hoverable">person</span> so struck,
he is liberated; there is no doubt of it.
Difficult to get is such a Guru who can
initiate <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">thus</span> by subtle impact; difficult <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">also</span> is
the disciple fit for i t ; it is only by happy
conjunction of merit that he is obtained But
this initiation <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> not be <span class="t1 t2 t4 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">given</span> to anybody and
everybody; such is the Command.
Duly worshipping the circle of the Kula with
appropriate ingredients of Kula worship, the
Guru <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> show it to the disciple. This is the
kauliki diksa, initiation of the Kaula.
Filling the mouth with the substance for
worship mixed with the five nectarous products
of the cow*, the Guru <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">shall</span> bathe the disciple
with i t ; this is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> the gandusa dkisa, mouthful initiation.
Diksa is again twofold depending on whether
it is external, bahya, or internal, antara; the
external is kriya diksa (ritualistic initiation) and
the other, internal, is the vedha diksa (subtle
impact).
Purification is twofold, inner and o u t e r ; the
inner is effected by appropriate ritual, the outer
by diksa. By diksa, the <span class="t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t13 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">light</span> of liberation, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">even</span>
the lowest born is freed. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Without</span> these <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">two</span> the
Kaulika is not liberated.

The <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> as such <span class="t1 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t19 t20 t21 t23 t24 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">cannot</span> be purified; nor the
karma. It is the inner being that is to be
processed through the diksa of the ageless Shakti
that is Kundali.
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Though</span> the ritual be the same, these dlksas
<span class="t0 t2 t3 t5 t7 t10 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t21 t24 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">work</span> out <span class="t1 t2 t18 t25 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">different</span> results on the meeting of the
Guru and the worthy disciple.
As the <span class="t0 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">power</span> of poison is killed by Mantra
or by medicine, so does the knower of Mantra
sever in a trice the bonds of the pasu by dlksa
From this extensive bondage diksa alone
liberates, by pointing out the supreme station
and leads to the ancient <span class="t0 t6 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t15 t16 t17 t20 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">divine</span> Abode.
Diksa, <span class="t1 t2 t4 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">given</span> <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t17 t18 t19 t21 t22 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">according</span> to the prescribed
mode, burns up in a moment all ill-omens and
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">great</span> sins in their millions.
That by which the pasus (animal men) have
their eyes opened and <span class="t8 t13 hoverable">become</span> Shivas, is the diksa
which liberates from the bonds of the paSus.
That which instantly generates faith and
conviction is diksa; the rest are only pleasing to
the populace.
That diksa <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> which there is no fulfil
ment <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">even</span> with a hundred upasanas, should be
obtained from a <span class="t4 t5 t8 t10 t11 t12 t15 t19 t20 t23 t25 hoverable">holy</span> Guru for the success of the
Mantra.
As iron struck by mercury becomes gold so
does the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">soul</span> struck by diksa attain to Shivahood
With all karma burnt out by diksat all bonds
of Maya severed, attaining to the supreme <span class="t7 t10 t15 t25 hoverable">end</span> of
Jnana, seedless*, he becomes Shiva.
Gone is the shudrahood of a shudra the
brahmanhood of a brahmana; there obtains no
distinction of caste where there is the effect of

PURASCHARANA*
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Among</span> the various lines of self-elevation
prescribed to the seekers of the Truth, the
Kularnava lauds the Japa as the pre-eminent and
invests it with the sanctity and efficacy of a
yajna, sacrifice, for attaining the fourfold object
of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span> viz. dharma, Right, artha, Wealth, Kama,
Desire and moksa, liberation. All other <span class="t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t9 t13 t14 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">means</span>
can be left out and only the <span class="t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t9 t13 t14 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t28 t29 hoverable">means</span> of mantra i.e.
japa of mantra resorted to which is sure to yield
success if carried out <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">without</span> blemish But if it
is allowed to be tarnished with fault then its
fruit is indeed inauspicious. Japa is the happy
giver of enjoyment, salvation, self-fulfilling
wish. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> practise the Yoga of Japa and
Dhyana. All blemishes due to transgressions of
rule, from the Jiva up to the Brahma, done knowingly or unknowingly, are wiped <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t20 t21 t22 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">away</span> by Japa.
Should you desire fulfilment in this <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span>
ridden heavily with unhappiness, doing Japa of
the Mantra with the five-limbed upasana you
w i l l attain happiness. Daily puja at the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span>
prescribed hours - in the morning, noon and
evening - japa, tarpana (offering of libation),
homa and feeding the Brahmanas is this fivefold
upasana <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> purascarana.
If any of these
limbs are lacking, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">make</span> up for it with appropriate increase of Japa as prescribed. For no
fulfilment is possible if there be want of l i m b ;
hence attempt to <span class="t1 t2 t4 t7 t15 t17 t18 t19 hoverable">set</span> it <span class="t27 hoverable">right</span> by Japa w i t h
devotion.

the b o d y ' and 'bathing the entire b o d y ' in the

Whatever action is done by <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> who is purified

by the tigers.

Japa is of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> kinds Japa done aloud in
the hearing of <span class="t1 t7 t13 hoverable">others</span> is the lowest; japa done in

extended, it causes decay of tapas; and when

There are ten processes for the eradication
of these defects of Mantra: giving birth, giving
life, striking making aware, ceremonial bath,
cleansing of i m p u r i t y , satisfying, libation,
lighting, covering in protection. As weapons
rubbed on the whetstone get sharpened, Mantras
subjected to these processes acquire bloom.
For <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> who does the mantra-japa the Sastra
lays down what is to be eaten, what is to be
offered, the vegetable, roots, fruit, barley etc.
If any <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> acquires merit in the w a y of the

from another, then half the merit belongs to the
donor of the food and half to the doer. <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Therefore</span> an intelligent <span class="t9 hoverable">person</span> shall, with all effort,

performance and of ritual for desired ends.
T h e tongue is burnt by the food of a n o t h e r ;
hands burnt by accepting from a n o t h e r ; the
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> burnt by (thoughts of) women of o t h e r s ;
how then can there be success in the endeavour?
If the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> be in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> place, Shiva (passive consciousness) in another, Shakti (active consciousness) in another, and life-breath in still <span class="t0 t1 t2 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t18 t19 t21 t23 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">another</span>

be gathered in <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> effort If learning is acquired
for the sake of debate, japa is done for the sake of
another, gifts <span class="t1 t2 t4 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">given</span> for the sake of fame, how can
there be fulfilment? If pilgrimage is done for the
sake of wealth, austerities for show, worship of
deity for selfish purpose, how indeed can there
be fulfilment? Fools are they who do nyasa,
puja, japa, homa, w i t h a <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">body</span> that is u n c l e a n ;
they all are fruitless. If the ritual is done by

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> unclean due to faces, urine and other
leavings, then all japa, worship etc. is rendered
i m p u r e . Him who makes japa with soiled cloth,
soiled hair, bad odour of mouth on his person,
the Deity being disgusted burns up in a moment.
Avoid during japa all laziness, yawning, sleep,
sneeze, spitting, fear, touching of lower limbs,
anger The mantra does not succeed where there
is excessive food, meaningless talk, gossip,
rigidity of rule, attachment to another, fickleness. Do not perform japa with a turban on,
w i t h cloak, naked, hair dishevelled, surrounded
by retinue, unclean upper cloth, or while i m p u r e
or while walking Avoid during Japa inertia,
grief, useless activity, free imagination and
passing of wind. Be calm, be clean, limited in
food, sleeping on ground, devoted, in full
control, free from duality, steady of mind,
silent, self-controlled and do Japa. With
confidence, belief, composure, faith, regularity,
certitude, contentment, enthusiasm, and <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span>
qualities, do Japa.
Success in japa lies in his hands who is
decked with fragrant flowers, ornaments and
clothes. Devoted to the Mantra, with <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">life</span>
dedicated to it, with <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> centred <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> it,
w h o l l y <span class="t1 t2 t4 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">given</span> to it, following its <span class="t6 t13 t14 t25 t27 hoverable">meaning</span> and
meditating <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> it, do Japa of the Mantra.
When tired by japa, <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">take</span> to dhyana; tired in
dhyana <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">take</span> again to japa. Of him who does
both japa and dhyana, the Mantra achieves anon.

APPENDIX A

<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t8 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 hoverable">WORD</span> - EXPLANATIONS
The seventeenth and the last Ullasa of the
Kularnava gives interesting derivations of <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">many</span>
of the important t e r m s in the Tantra Sastra
throwing a flood of <span class="t1 t2 t3 t4 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t13 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">light</span> on the height of aim
and the exactitude in detail of the wide-visioned
builders of this system. It begins with the Gurumantra, the prayer to the Guru:
" B o w to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thee</span> Oh Lord, to Shiva in the <span class="t6 t7 t8 t9 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span>
of the Guru, who takest on <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">many</span> forms for the
purpose of the manifestation and the fulfilment
of the supreme Knowledge; who art in the <span class="t6 t7 t8 t9 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span>
of Narayana, who art in the <span class="t6 t7 t8 t9 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> of the supreme
Self, who art the <span class="t0 t8 t11 t14 t23 t25 t28 hoverable">sun</span> dispelling the darkness of
all Ignorance, who art charged with cit, who
knowest all, who a r t the embodiment of compassion, who art the Auspicious. who givest
w h a t is auspicious to all devotees here and
beyond.
I bow to <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Thee</span> in front, at the sides, at
the back, above and below. As Sat-Chit, ordain
that I m a y <span class="t29 hoverable">ever</span> be T h y servitor.
Guru: gu signifies darkness; ru what restrains it. He who restrains darkness (of ignorance) is the guru.
ga signifies giver of fulfilment; r, severer of
s i n ; u, Vishnu. He who contains all the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">three</span> in
himself is the supreme guru.
ga signifies wealth of knowledge; r, illumin a t o r ; u, identity with Shiva- He who contains
these in himself is the guru.

Acarya: He conducts, carate, <span class="t0 t1 t3 t4 t5 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t17 t18 t19 t21 t22 t24 t26 t27 t29 hoverable">according</span> to

he is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> the acarya.

Aradhya:
Because he gives the consciousness of Self, atmabhava, because he has rejected
likes and dislikes, ragadvesa, and because his
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t24 t25 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">mind</span> is centred solely in meditation, dhyana, he
is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> araahya.
Desika:
Because he wears the <span class="t6 t7 t8 t9 t13 t14 t16 t17 t19 t20 t21 t28 t29 hoverable">form</span> of the
deity, devata, because he bestows grace on the
disciple, Sisya, and because he is the embodiment of compassion, karuna, he is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> desika.
Svami:
Because he exudes his inner,
svanta, peace, and deliberates on the supreme
truth, and because he is devoid of false
knowings, mithyajnana, he is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> svami.
Mahesvara:
Because he is devoid of the
blemishes of mind, manodosa, etc., becuse he
rejects dry argument and the like, hetuvada,
because of his likeness to animals <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">like</span> dogs,
Svadi, and because he is pleasing, ramya, he is
<span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> Mahes'vara.
Srinatha:
Because he imparts the <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">knowledge</span>
of prosperity, sri, and liberation, because he instructs on Nada <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Brahman</span> and Atman, and
because he is an emblem of the blocking,
sthagita, of Ignorance, he is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> Srinatha.
Deva: Because he crosses the bounds of
Space and Time, desakala, because he has

the Jiva, he is <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">called</span> Deva.

Prabhu: Because he deliberates <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">upon</span> the

Samyami: Because he rejects misery due to

p r e v i o u s b i r t h s , purvajanma, b e c a u s e i t p r e v e n t s
b i r t h s a n d d e a t h s , janmamrtyu, b e c a u s e i t y i e l d s
c o m p l e t e f r u i t , it is c a l l e d puja.
Arcana: B e c a u s e i t
yields the
desired
fruit,
abhistaphala,
h o l d s the fruit of a l l the
f o u r classes, caturvarga,
a n d d e l i g h t s , randanat,
a l l t h e gods, it is c a l l e d arcana.
Tarpana:
B e c a u s e t o t h e <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">God</span> t h a t i s t h e
Truth,
tattva,
s u r r o u n d e d b y His r e t i n u e ,
parivara,
it g i v e s n i n e f o l d d e l i g h t , navananda,
it is c a l l e d tarpana.
Gandha:
B e c a u s e it d e s t r o y s t h e affliction
of m i s f o r t u n e , d e e p a n d b o u n d l e s s , gambhira,
b e c a u s e it g i v e s k n o w l e d g e of dharma, it is
c a l l e d gandha.
Amoda:
B e c a u s e it c a u s e s t h e b i r t h of a l l
t h a t is b a s e d on S m e l l a g h r a n a n a (i.e. tattva, of
prithivi),
shows
the
path
of
salvation,
moksamarga,
s u b j u g a t e s a l l c u r s e d g r i e f etc.,
daghdaduhkha, it is c a l l e d amoda.
Aksata:
B e c a u s e t h e y y i e l d food,
anna,
e l i m i n a t e c o m p l e t e l y , ksapita, a l l s i n , a n d m a k e
o n e identified w i t h T h a t ( t r u t h ) Tat, t h e y a r e
c a l l e d aksata.
Puspa:
B e c a u s e it i n c r e a s e s m e r i t , punya,
r e m o v e s the heap of sin, papa, y i e l d m u c h
wealth,
puskalartha,
it is c a l l e d puspa.
Dhupa:
Because it drives out c o m p l e t e l y ,

Because

Tattvatraya:
By m e r e service to the <span class="t0 t6 t7 t10 t11 t12 t13 t15 t16 t17 t20 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">Divine</span>

Caluka:

it is c a l l e d caluka.
Prasada:
Because i t y i e l d s a n a n d a i n t h e
f o r m of L i g h t , prakasa, b e c a u s e it y i e l d s h a r m o n y , s a m a r a s y a , a n d b e c a u s e i t r e v e a l s , darsana
t h e S u p r e m e T r u t h , i t i s c a l l e d praSada.
Pana:
Because it s e v e r s t h e b o n d s , paSat
p r e v e n t s h e l l , naraka, a n d b e c a u s e i t p u r i f i e s ,
pavanat,
it is c a l l e d pana.

KULARNAVA TANTRA

Upasti:
S e r v i c e a t close q u a r t e r s a s p r e s cribed, by action, by mind, by speech, in all
s t a t e s is c a l l e d upasti.
Purascarana:
B e c a u s e it is d e a r to t h e
chosen Deity
by reason of its five-limbed
a d o r a t i o n , it l e a d s in f r o n t of t h e d e v o t e e , purah
caratit it is c a l l e d purascarana
Arghya:
B e c a u s e it d e s t r o y s a l l s i n , aghat
because it increases wealth and
progeney,
b e c a u s e i t y i e l d s p r i c e l e s s f r u i t , anargha-phala,
it is c a l l e d arghya.
A n d finally, t h e ksetra, t h e s a c r e d Centre of
devotions is not a n y <span class="t0 t1 t2 t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">one</span> particular <span class="t3 t4 t5 t6 t7 t8 t9 t10 t11 t12 t13 t14 t15 t16 t17 t18 t19 t20 t21 t22 t23 t24 t25 t26 t27 t28 t29 hoverable">place</span> but
A l l t h i s t h a t i s m o b i l e a n d i m m o b i l e , etatcaracaram
sarvam; He w h o g u a r d s , p r o t e c t s
t h i s A l l i s t h e ksetrapala, t h e s u p r e m e G u a r d .
